concept-created: {2018-07-01}

description of U+16800..U+16A3F

description::
· Unicode-block-name= Bamum-Supplement
· range= U+16800|92160|𖠀..U+16A3F|92735|𖨿
· plane= plane.1

· quantity-of-chars= 569
· script= Bamum
